METHOD     (TOF  )    Time of flight, flight path about 100 m.    2011400100029 
            The n-flight path tube is inclined 9 deg with respect 2011400100030 
            to the normal to the moderator surface and is         2011400100031 
            interrupted at about 50 m where the 2-row 4-position  2011400100032 
            sample changer and two collimators are placed.        2011400100033 
           (TRN) Transmission method. (see comment).              2011400100034 
            Background was determined by "black resonance" method.2011400100035 
            Additional background samples to determine shape of   2011400100036 
            background  were inserted in third run which followed 2011400100037 
            each "sample-in", "sample-out" sequence.              2011400100038
